The acharya institute of technology is a technological university affiliated with visvesvaraya technological university, located in india, specifically in bangalore, karnataka. it was established in the year 2000 and is currently directed by dr. g.p. prabhukumar. the campus is situated at "in soldevanahalli, acharya dr. sarvapalli radhakrishnan road, hessarghatta main road, bangalore – 560090." visvesvaraya technological university is headquartered in belgaum.
